 
KWAFA GULA LINAMASI (Things Fall Apart) 
Isihloko sesiNgisi: Things Fall Apart Umbhali: Chinua Aehebe Umdwebi-zithombe: Uehe Okeke Umhumushi: C.T. Msimang 
,  
 
 INGXENYE YOKUQALA
 

 
ISAHLUKO 1 
U-OKonkwo wabe engusaziwayo ezigodini ezingaphezulu kweziyisishiyagalolunye. Lolu dumo olungaka wayezizuzele lona ngempumelelo yakhe luqobo. Ngesikhathi eseyibhungu elineminyaka eyishumi nesishiyagalombili nje kuphela, wahlabanela isigodi sakubo ngokunqoba u-Amalinze owayebizwa ngokuthi yiMpaka. U-Amalinze lona kwakuyinkunzimalanga yesigonyagonya okwase kuphele iminyaka eyisikhombisa edla ubhedu kwezokugonyozana kusuka e-Umuofia kuze kuyoshaya koMbaino imbala. Kwakuthiwa nguMpaka ngakho ngoba wayesho kahle athi akayi phansi engendlalelwe. Naphezu kunjalo, u-Okonkwo wayiginqa phansi Ie nsizwa empini eyesabekayo, lapho kwayena ufeleba lona wavuma ukuthi wayengakaze ayibone impi enzima kangako selo umsunguli wedolobha lakubo atholana phezulu nomoya wasendle izinsuku eziyisikhombisa nobusuku obuyisikhombisa. 
    Hhayi-ke! Kwaduma izigubhu, kwankeneneza imitshingo, izibukeli zona zabamba izibindi ngezandla. Phela u-Amalinze wayelwisa okwengwe yehlathi, kanti u-Okonkwo yena wabe engunompunyumpunyu okwenhlanzi yamanzi. Zasiphalaza izinsizwa kwaqansa imithambo ezingalweni, einhlane, emathangeni, kangangokuthi kwakuba sengathi izogqashuka. Nokho ekugcineni u-Okonkwo wayigingqa phansi iMpaka. 
Nanxa kunjalo, lokhu sekuyiminyakanyaka kwenzeka. 
Gshe ukuthi sekwedlula iminyaka engamashuni amabili noma ngaphezulu kwenzeka lokhu. Kungaleso sikhathi lapho udumo luka-Okonkwo Iwabhebhetheka nezwe lonke kuhle komlilo wequbula. Umfo lona wayeyisigadla sensizwa, futhi esukile 



 
egadeni. Amashiya lana kwakungamashoba, ikhala kuyisinakanaka esigcwele bonke ubuso lobu, okwakwenza ukuba esabeke kakhulu. Wayephefumulela phezulu njalo nje, angiphathi-ke ebusuku, kwase kudume ukuthi abantabakhe kanye nesithembu sakhe babemuzwa ehona yize belele kwezinye izindlu. Wayehambela phezulu, acokame, izithende lezi ziwunyathele kancane umhlabathi. Kwakuba sengathi izinyawo lezi zinezipilingi, ahambe sengathi kukhona azombhozomela. Vele wayejwayele ukubabhozomela abantu bengazelele. Njengoba wayenamalimi nje, wayethi angathukuthela, acinane, izwi lingabe lisaphuma kahle, bese ebona ukuthi ngcono avele asebenzise inqindi. Wayengenaso nesincane isikhathi sezehluleki. Ngokunjalo wayengakwazi ukuzibekezelela. Uyise, ogama lakhe lingu-Anoka, kwase kwedlule iminyaka eyishumi ashona. Esaphila, wabe eyivila lendoda engakwazi nokucabangela ikusasa. Uma eke wathola imali, okuyinto eyayingavamile nokho, wayethenga izigubhu zobusula ameme omakhelwane, kuhlalwe phansi kuphuzwe. Wayehlale ethi njalo nxa ebona umlomo wendoda esishonile wayethola isifundo sokuthi kuwubulima obuphindiwe ukuba umuntu azincishe ukudla kukhona ngesikhathi esaphila, alibale wukuthi sibekelwa ngaphandle. Okudabukisayo nje wukuthi ezakhe izikweletu zazingangotshani. Akukho noyedwa komakhelwane bakhe ayengarnkweleti imali ethile kusuka kwencane kuya kwenkulu engamakhulukhulu amaKhawuri (noma izimbazu). 
Wayemude naye kodwa ewukhahla nje oluthe ukuqhotha. 
Ubuso bakhe babuhlala bubaqakile, budonsekile, ngaphandle kwalapho ethole amanzi amponjwana noma-ke ezishayela umtshingo wakhe. Phela wayeyingcweti ekushayeni umtshingo. Kanjalo-ke, isikhathi ayesenamela kakhulu yizinyanga ezimbili noma ezintathu ~ge~uva kokuvuna, okuyisikhathi lapho bonke abadlah-rrutshmgo babeyethula emigibeni engaphezu kwamaziko. 
    U-Unoka naye wayeba mdibi munye nabo ashaye owakhe naye umtshingo. Kulapho wawubona khona ubuso bakhe 
sebuchachambile, benanela lokhu kubusiseka kanye nokuthula. Kwesinye isikhathi abakwesinye isigodi babeye bameme u-Unoka neqembu lakhe lengoma kanye nawo-egwugwu abasina indlamu ukuba beze bazobadlalela futhi babafundise izingoma zabo. Babeye baye la bemenywe khona bafike badlale amakhonsathi kuze kuphele amasonto amathathu noma amane bezitika ngomculo nangezibiliboco. U-Unoka wayekujabulela ukungcebeleka kanye nobungani, ngakho wayehlala ethokozile kulesi sikhathi sonyaka lapho izimvula sezinqamukile nelanga selibalele kamnadi, kanti futhi kwakungashisi kangako ngoba kunenkwezane yomoya wenyakatho ohlabayo owawuvunguza ngaleso sikhathi. Ngezinye izikhathi wawuvunguza ngamandla impel a, ubone sekulele umlalamvubu nezwe seliyizintuli. Amakhehla 'nezingane wawungababona bengasasuki eziko, botha imbuthuma. Konke lokhu kwakumthozisa kakhulu u-Unoka, ejabulela nokubuya kwawonhloyile bebika ukuphela kwezimvula, abantwana nabo becula bengaphezi, bethakasela ukubuya kwalezi zinyoni. Omdala way eye akhumbule naye eseyingane, ezingelana nonhloyile, efuna ukubabona bendiza bedabula umkhathi. Wayenele ayibone Ie nyoni acule ngenhliziyo yakhe yonke, ejabulela ukubuya kwayo kwezinde izinkalo, eyibuza futhi ukuthi ngabe imphathele yini imidweshu yezindwangu. 
    Yindaba endala-ke leyo, no-Unoka eseyingane. Wathi angakhula, waphenduka esesabekayo isehluleki. Wayempofu kangangoba umndeni wakhe wawuke untule ngisho okuya ethunjini. Abantu babemhleka usulu ngokulova kwakhe etnsebenzini, futhi babefunga begomela bethi abasayuphinde bameboleke imali ngoba akabe esababuyisela. Kodwa-ke u-Unoka kwakuyindoda enolimi. Yayithi ingazjncengela, iphume iqhasha imali sebemeboleka futhi, kwaba wukunqwabelana kwezikweletu-ke lokho. 
    Lusuku lumbe umakhelwane wakhe ongu-Okoye wamvakashela. Wamfica eshaye amanhlakomuzi omdala, embhedeni wakhe webumba, ezishayela umtshingo wakhe. Wavuka khona manjalo waxhawula ku-Okoye owathi

angabamba ithambo wayesendlala isikhumba sembuzi ayesigodle ekhwapheni, wayesehlala phansi. U-Unoka wangena ekamelweni, waphuma nogqoko olwalunesigaxa sekhola, neqhuzwana likapelepele kanye nesinqamu sikashoki. 
    "Nansi ikhola," kubika u-Unoka edlulisela ugqoko osivakashini sakhe qede ehlala phansi. 
"Ngiyabonga. Lowo okupha ikhola usuke ekupha impilo. 
Nokho ngicabanga ukuthi kufanele usihlephule isigaxa," kusho u-Okoye eluphindisela emuva ugqoko. 
    "Qha, ngikupha yona," baphikisana kanjalo kwaze kwathi ekugcineni wasemukela isicelo s.okuba kube nguyena osihlephulayo isigaxa. Ngaso leso sikhathi u-Okoye wathatha isinqamu sikashoki, wadweba imigqa embalwa phansi endlini, wayesezipenda kuqukula. Ngenkathi esihlephula isigaxa, u-Unoka wabe ethetha amadlozi, ecela impilo enhle, ukuphepha emikhuhlaneni, nokuvikeleka ezitheni zabo. Bathe bangadla bathi du, baxoxa ngalokhu nangalokhuya, ikakhulukazi ngezimvula ezase zigcugcisa amabhoqongwana emasimini, nangomkhosi wabaphansi owawususeduze kanye nempi eyayifunwa ngabaseMbaino. U-Unoka wayengakhululeki nakancane nxa sekuxoxwa ezempi. Empeleni wayeyivaka, esaba ngisho ukulibheka igazi. Kanjalo washes he wayishintsha inkulumo wayesexoxa ngomculo, lapho wawubona ngezihlathi nje sezivakashela amadlebe. Kwakuba sengathi uyezwa ngendlebe yengqondo, isiqgi esisusa usinga sezingoma ze-ekwa, ne-udu kanye ne-ogene, kube sengathi useyawuzwa nomtshingo wakhe usuzicwenga ngobunono bekati kuqubuka imvunge yosizi. Lokhu kwakunomphumela othokozisayo futhi ozwakala masishane, kodwa okuthi lapho uwulandela kahle umtshingo, uya phansi phezulu, bese ushaya imvunge enezikhawu, umuntu wayezwa olukhulu usizi nokudabuka lapho. 
    U-Okoye naye wabe engumculi. Yena wayeshaya i-ogene, okuwuhlobo oluthile lwesitolotolo. Nokho wayengesona isehluleki njengo-Unoka. Eyakhe inqolobane yayigcwele amabhoqongwana kanti futhi wayenesithembu samakhosikazi 
amathathu. Futhi wayesecothele ukuba azuze isicoco esibizwa ngokuthi yi-idemili, okungesesithathu kweziphakeme kakhulu kulelo zwe. Kwakuzoba ngumgidi onezindleko ezinkulu ngakho wayehamba eqokelela zonke izikweletu zakhe. Nalapha kwa-Unoka wayelethwe yilokho-ke. Wathi ukushaya isikhwehlela wayeseluqala udaba eze ngalo: "Ume njalo ngekhola. Nokho ngethemba ukuthi usuke wezwa ngesicoco engisigaqele." 
    Nanxa inkulumo yakhe wayeyicacisile phambilini, emva kwalokho u-Okoye wayishubisa inkulumo elandelanisa izaga ezaze zaba yisithupha. Phela esizweni sama-Tho ubugagu bokukhuluma yinto eyigugu kabi. Izaga lezi zithathwa njengesishebo esinandisa ink:ulumo, ishelele kamnandi. U-Okoye lona wayeyigagu futhi ekhuluma elule. Wayeqale ayendlalele kahle inkulumo yakhe ngaphambi kokuba angene sm kuyo. Kafushane nje lapha wayenxusa ukuba u-Unoka ambuyisele amakhulu amabili amaKhawri okwase kuphele iminyaka emibili emkweleta wona. Kwathi angezwa u-Unoka ukuthi umngani wakhe uze ngani, wahleka waze waqethuka. Wahleka wagegetheka isikhathi eside izwi lakhe lizwakala ngokucacile okungathi kukhala isitolotolo. Buka ngoba wahleka waze wachiphiza izinyembezi imbala. Isivakashi samane sakhungatheka nje. Ekugcineni waphendula u-Unoka kodwa esalokhu ehleka izihatha njalo nje. 
    "Bheka laphaya obondeni," esho ekhomba udonga lwendlu oluthe qekelele, olwalucakwe ngensoyi Iwaze Iwacwebezela. "Bheka leyo midwebo kashoki," nebala u-Okoye wawabona amaqoqo emidwa kashoki isuka phansi iya phezulu. Yayidwetshwe yaba ngamaqoqo amahlanu. Iqoqo eHncane kunawo onke lalinemigqa elishumi. U-Unoka kwakuyindoda ethandayo ukudumelisa, ngako wathi ukuthula, wathi buku ugwayi eshungwini lakhe wabhema. Wathimula kabi1i kathathu ngaphambi kokuba aqhubeke. "Yilelo nalelo qoqo kulana limele umuntu othile engimkweletayo, kanti-ke futhi umugqa ngamunye umele ikhulu lamaKhawri. Uyazibonela-ke nawe ukuthi leya ndoda ngiyikweleta inkulungwane yonke.

Yize kunjalo ibingakangihlaseli intathakusa izongiphazamisa ngoba nje isifuna ngiyikhokhele. Ngizokukhokhela, kodwa-ke hhayi narnhlanje. Phela babengaqambi manga abadala uma bethi ilanga likhanyisa abemile ngaphambi kokuba likhanyise abaguqe ngaphansi kwabo. Ngizokhokhela kuqala labo engibakweleta imali eningi. "Waphinda wancinza kancane eshungwini lakhe, wabhema. Umuntu wayengaze acabange ukuthi ukubhema lokhu iyona ndlela okukhokhwa ngayo izikweletu ezinkulu kuqala. U-Okoya wagoqa isikhumba sakhe sembuzi, zaya. 
    Waze washona u-Unoka engazange azuze ngisho esisodwa isicoco, kuphela nje izikweletu zakhe zazingangoboya benkomo. Akumangalisi-ke ukuthi indodana yakhe, u-Ukonkwo wayenamahloni ngoyise. Ngenhlahla kulesi sizwe umuntu wayengahlulelwa ngokuthi uzalwa ngubani, kepha ngokuthi yena ungubani. U-Okonkwo kwakungabuzwa nakubuzwa ukuthi unesiphiwo sezinto emphakathini. Narum ayesernncane, wayeseyindumandumane ezweni ngokuhlabana kwakhe kwezokugonyoza ezigodini eziyisishiyagalolunye. Wayengumlimi odla kusale, izingorna zakhe ezimbili zigcwele phama amabhoqongwana kanti wayesanda kusinelwa ngumlobokazi wesithathu. Okukhulu kakhulu wukuthi wayesezuze izicoco ezimbili futhi ekhombise ukuhlabana okwesabekayo izimpini phakathi kwezizwe ezingomakhelwane. Yize ayesemncane, wayesethathwa njengothulasizwe endaweni. Abantu abadala babehlonishwa ezweni lakubo kodwa izingwazi zazikhulekelwa. Nesaga sakhona sasikufakazela lokhu ngoba sasithi uma ingane ikwazi ukugeza izandla ingadla namakhosi. Wayesenjalo-ke u-Okonkwo ngesikhathi kunikelwa ngensizwa ethile kwabase-Umoufia, inikelwa ngomakhelwane ukuze kunqandwe impi nokuchitheka kwegazi. Leyo nsizwa eyayibhekwe yisambane kwabe kungu-Ikemefuna.

ISAHLUKO 2 
U-Okonkwo wayeqeda ukucisha isiphefu, esazelula karnnandi embhedeni wakhe woqalo ngenkathi ezwa i-ogene yenhlabamkhosi yakuleso sifunda yenanela ezinzulwini zobusuku. Gome, gome, gome, isho iphindelela. Emva kwalokho inhlabarnkhosi yawefhula urnlayezo wayo. Nanku lowo mbiko. Leyo naleyo ndoda kwakumele iye enkundleni ekuseni ngosuku olulandelayo. Wamane wamangala nje u-Okonkwo ukuthi kazi kwenzenjani, kodwa ezwa ngisho ~gazini nje ukuthi konakele e-Umuofia. Yayizwakala nje mhlabamkhosi ukuthi isho ngelosizi, elalilokhu lizwakala lenanelwa ngamagagasi omoya yize seyedlulile inhlabarnkhosi. 
    Kwakuthule du ngalobo busuku. Imvama kwakuhlale kuthule ngaphandle kwalapho kuqhakaze unyezi. Uma kurnnyarna abantu babesaba kuze kwesabe ngisho iziqhwaga imbala. Izingane zazidonswa ngendlebe kuthiwe zingalokothi zishaye amakhwelo ebusuku ngoba kwesatshwa irnimoya emibi. Nezilwane eziyingozi kwakubasengathi zibikezela ingozi enkulu ebusuku. Inyoka lena yayingagagulwa ngegama ebusuku, kwesatshwa ukuthi izokuzwa. Yayibizwa ngokuthi usinga. Ngakho-ke kulobu busuku lathi lingantongoloza lithathwe ngumoya izwi lenhlabarnkhosi, kwagunya u,kuthula okwesabekayo kwasala urnsindo wezihlonono kuphela. 
    Ukuba kwakunonyezi kwakuyobangconywana. Kwakuyobe kuzwakaIa narnazwana arnnandi ezingane ngenkathi zizidIaIela ernasirnini. MhIawumbe intsha nayo yayizobe iwubucwibi obuhle obuhamba ngabubili, ingcebelekile. Izalukazi namakhehla kwakuzobe kubalisa ngezinsuku ezedlulayo. Kakade isisho 




 
sama-Ibo sithi: "Uma kukhanya unyezi ngisho nesishosha silambela ukuhamba." 
Ngeshwa-ke, ngalobu busuku kwakumnyama khuhle. 
Kuzo zonke izigodi zase -Umuofia eziyisishiyagalolunye, inhlabamkhosi yayilimise ngesihloko, ishaya ne-ogeneyayo, ithi yileyo naleyo ndoda ifuneka enkundleni ngakusasa ekuseni. Ulele embhedeni woqalo nje u-Okonkwo uyazibuza uyaziphendula ukuthi ngabe ngesani lesi sidumo esingaka. Ngabe sekuthiwa ayihlome ihlasele iyodla omakhelwane? Waqina impela lowo mqondo kuyilapho-ke wayengayesabi neze impi. Wayeyibutho futhi eyindoda ezibambelayo. Wayengamfuzanga uyise owayesaba ngisho ukulibheka igazi. Kwelase-Umuofia empini yokugcina ababeyilwile nguyena owayehlabane kuqala wabuya ephethe ikhanda lesitha. Leso sitha kwabe sekungumuntu wesihlanu ayesembulele yize ayesemncane. Ngemikhosi emikhulu njengemigubho kanye nemingcwabo obakhe utshwala wayebuphuzela ogebhezini Iwekhanda lendoda. 
    Kwathi kusa ngakusasa abantu base bephelele ngothi Iwabo enkundleni yasendalini. Cishe ukuthi amadoda ayelapho ayeyizinkulungwane eziyishumi, onke ekhulumela phansi. 
    Ngelikade u-Ogbuefi Ezeugo waphakama, wabhavumula . kwaze kwaba kane ethi: "Urnuofia kwenu" okungukuthi "Siyabingelela nina base-Umuofia." Usho njalo ude ebheka ngapha abuye abheke ngale macala onke, efumbethe inqindi okusengathi uxosha ngayo umoya. Wayebe esasho ukhukhulelangoqo wezinkulungwane zamadoda wenanele uthi: "Yebo:" Emva kwalokho kwaphinde kwathula kwathi duo U-Ogbuefi Ezeugo kwabe kuyimbongi eyaziwayo futhi emikhosini efana nalena kwakukhethwa yena ukuba ethule inkulumo. Wathi ukuphulula izinwele kanye nentshebe yakhe okwasekumhlophe wu. Wathi ukuzilungisa, ukuze izevatho zakhe zamahiya ayephuma phansi kwekhwapha athekelezwe ehlombe, ezoma ngononina. 
"Siyabingelela ma-Umuofia amahle," esebhavumula okwesihlanu, nebandla limenanela, livuma. Bengazelele, 
isandla saqhashisa okomcibisholo sakhomba ngaseMbaino, wakhuluma ehlanganise amazinyo, eququda imihlathi wathi: 
"Laya mankengane abe nesibindi sokubulala indodakazi yomu-Umuofia." Wathi ukukhothamisa ikhanda lelo eququda imihlathi njalo, kanti wenzela laba abavunganyiswa wukuthukuthela bezothula ngaphambi kokuba aqhubeke. Ngenkathi eseqhubeka, igwebu lolaka lase lehlile, esemamatheka kancane, kodwa kubonakala ukhuthi uhleka inhlinini. Okwakuyinto eyethusa ukwedlula ukukhombisa kwakhe intukuthelo. Wachaza kahle-ke manje ukuthi indodakazi yase-Umuofia ibulawe kanjani ngenkathi ihambele kwelaseMbaino iyothenga. Wachaza futhi ukuthi lowo bekuyinkosikazi ka-Ogbuefi Udo, esho eyikhomba leyo ndoda eyayigebise ikhanda ihlezi ecakwakhe. Ibandla lamemeza ngolaka olukhulu selomele igazi. 
    Baningi abakhulumayo emva kwalokho, kodwa bagcina bevumelene ngokuthi akuqhutshwe ngosiko olwaziwayo. Kusho ukuthi kwathunyelwa isigijimi eMbaino kuthiwa abakhethe phakathi kokuba ibambane ngezihluthu nokuba banikele ngebhungu netshitshi labo kube umhlabelo. 
Omakhelwane babesesaba isigodi sase-Umuofia. 
Sasinamandla empini nakwezemilingo. Kanti futhi izinyanga nezangoma zakhona zazesatshwa ezweni lonke. Izintelezi zakhona zokuchela impi ibe namandla kwase kuyinto endalandala yakhona. Akekho owayengasho ukuthi zaqala nini ukusetshenziswa lezo zintelezi. Kunye ababekwazi futhi bevumelana ngako bonke, ukuthi emandulo umuthi lona kwabe kuyinkosikazi end ala, emlenzemunye. Empeleni umuthi wawubizwa ngokuthi yi-agadi-nwayi noma isalukazi esidala. lmithi yayakhelwe indlu yayo phakathi nomuzi wase-Umuofia, endaweni ecatshwe kahle. Lowo owenze ubulima nokungahloniphi, wedlula kuleyo ndawo sekuhlwile nakanjani wayembona umlenzemunye egxumagxuma. 
    Yilokho-ke izizwe ezingomakhelwane, ezazikwazi konke lokhu ngama-Umuofia, zazingeke zivume kalula ukuba ishayane ngezifuba, kwakungamane kuxoxiswane ngenhloso

yokuthelelana amanzi. Singasho singahlonizi ukuthi nembala abase-Umuofia babengalokothi bahlasele ngaphambi kokuba bazenelise ukuthi isizathu sempi sisobala futhi sifanele kangangoba ngisho lowo ongumlomo kaMvelinqangi uyasemukela. Sisho phela uSomlomo wamagquma nemigede. Phela zikhona izikhathi lapho uSomlomo wayeke abenqabele abase-Umuofia ukuba bahlasele. Uma isizwe singamhloniphi sasifike sinqotshwe empini, ngoba phela intelezi yabo enkulu yayingayilwi impi enokusola kwabase-Ibo. 
    Nokho-ke lena eyabe isinyathele amasimba abantwana kwabe kuyimpi efanele ukuliwa. Ngisho nazo izitha zazikwazi lokho. Kanjalo-ke kwathi lapho u-Okonkwo umu-Umuofia efika eMbaino ngesithunzi sakhe sasebukhosini ezothi abaphisele, wemukelwa ngenkulu inhlonipho, wabungazwa izinsuku ezimbili phambi kokuba aphindele emuva eseqhuba ibhungu eliminyaka iyishumi-nanhlanu kanye netshitshi. Igama lebhungu lelo kwakungu-Ikemefuna, okuye kuthi lapho ama-Umuofia exoxa indaba yakhe edabukisayo uwabone ehIengezela izinyembezi ngisho nanamuhIa lokhu. 
    Izingwevu ezibizwa futhi ngokuthi ama-ndichie zahlangana zizokuzwa umbiko ka-Okonkwo mayelana nohambo lwakhe. Ekugcineni zathatha isinqumo esasivele silindelekile, sokuba itshitshi libe ngumka-Ogbuefi, ukuze kuvuke indlu yomkakhe owayebulewe. Ibhungwana lona kwathiwa ngelesizwe sonke, ngakho akusheshanga ukuthathwa kwesinqumo sokuthi kuzokwenziwani ngalo. Kuphela kwanqunywa ukuba ligcinwe nguye u-Okonkwo aligcinele isizwe okwesikhashana. Nangempela kwaphela iminyaka emithathu qolokonqo u-Ikemefuna ehlala ernzini ka-Okonkwo. 
    U-Okonkwo lona umuzi wakhe wayewuphethe ngesandla esiqotho. Amakhosikazi akhe ikakhulukazi isincanekazana, kanye nabantabakhe kwakumesabisa okwemamba ngenxa yolaka ayenalo. Kungenzeka nokho ukuthi empeleni wayengeyena umuntu onolaka. Iqiniso wukuthi impilo yonke yakhe yabe ibuswa wukwesaba; esaba ukuba yisehluIeki nokuba buthakathaka. Lokhu 
kwesaba kwakujule ukwedlula ngisho ukwesaba imimoya emibi nabathakathi. KwedIuIa ngisho ukwesaba izinto zemvelo njengamahlathi nezilwane ezihlale zihogela igazi. Kwakungekhona ukwesaba izinto ezingaphandle ezibonwa ngabantu kepha kujuIe ngaphakathi. Wayeze azesabe kwayena siqu. Esaba ukuthi angahle afuze uyise. Ngisho esengumfanyana wayekuzonda ukwehIuIeka nobuthakathaka bukayise. Ingani kuze kubemanje nje akakakhohIwa yihlazo alithelwa yiloya mfanyana ababedlala naye besebancane, owamthuka ngokuthi uyise yi-agbala, okungukuthi yinina. Wayeqala ukuzwa u-Dkonkwo ukuthi kanti nabesilisa bake babizwe ngokuthi bangamanina njengabantu besifazane uma nje bengakaze bahIabane. 
    Inye-ke into eyayibusa u-Okonkwo, wukuba azonde yonke into eyabe ithandwa nguyise u-Unoka. Okunye kwalezo zinto kwabe kungukuthamba nobuvila. 
    Ngokwethwasa kwehlobo u-Okonkwo walima ngokukhulu ukukhuthala, eqala ukukhala kwezinkukhu aze alanyulelwe wukuhwalala. Kwakuyisigadla sendoda esebenza ingakhathali. Ngeshwa isithembu sakhe nabantwana bona babengaqinile njengaye ngakho umsebenzi wawubakhandla. Nokho babengeke bathi vu ngalokho. Indodana yakhe endala, uNwoye wayeseneminyaka eyishumi nambili, kodwa eseqalile ukudumaza uyise ngobuvila, uma sibuka ngeso likayise, owayezama ukumfaka endleleni ngokumkhankatha nokumdixa ngenduku. Kwabonakala nje ukuthi 10 mntwana ukhula kabuhIungu, usizi lubhalwe kuye ebusweni. 
    Ukuthi u-Dkonkwo umi kahIe kwakubonakala ngisho ernzini wakhe. Wayenenxuluma elikhulu elibiyelwe ngodonga olubanzi lwenhlabathi ebomvu. Indlu yakhe okuthi'Ya yi-obi, yayakhiwe ngemuva kancane kwesango, okwakuwukuphela kwalo kulezi zindonga ezibomvu. Yilowo nalowo kubafazi bakhe wayenendlu yakhe, zonke zakhe isigubudu ngemuva kwe-obi. Inqolobane yona yayakhiwe yeyama ngodonga lothango. Yayinodlame lwezingodo okwakugcanywe kulo amabhoqongwana. Kule ngxenye engapha yomuzi

kwakunesibaya sezimbuzi, kanti leyo naleyo nkosikazi yayizakhele elayo ihhoko lezinkukhu. Eduze nenqolobal)e kwakunendlwana yabaphansi encanyana. Yindlu lena eyayihlala imithi kanye nezinto ezibaziwe akhonza ngazo abaphansi. Wayebakhonza ngokubanikelela ngezinhlamvu zekhola, nokudla, kanye namanzi amponjwana. Kanti futhi wayengakuyekile ukubathandaza, ezithandazela yena namakhosikazi akhe amathathu kanye nezingane zakhe eziyisishiyagalombili. 
    Ngakho-ke ngesikhathi okwabulawa ngaso owesifazane wase-Umuofia eMbaino, u-Ikemefuna weza emzini ka-Okonkwo. Ngesikhathi emIetha ekhaya u-Okonkwo wabiza umkakhe omdala wathi nguyena okumele agcine lowo mfana. "Ungowesizwe sonke," kuchaza u-Okonkwo. "Ngakho kumele umqaphele." 
"Ngabe sizomgcina isikhathi eside yini?" kubuza umkakhe. "Yenza engikutshela khona, mfazi ndini," kubhavumula u-Okonkwo, engenwa ngamalimi. "Kuqale nini ukuba nawe ube yingwevu lapha e-Umuofia?" Nempela-ke unina kaNwoye walithatha ibhungwana waligcina engasaphindanga ukubuza eminye imibuzo. 
    Ibhungwana lona lalivevezela wuvalo. Lalingazi ukuthi livelelwa yini, nokuthi loneni. Lalingazi noma uyise nguyena yini obulele owesimame wase-Umuofia. Akwaziyo nje wukuthi uyise wafika ekhaya namadoda ambalwa ayekhulumela phansi, kanti ekugcineni azomnikela kulo mfokazi. Unina yena wakhihla isililo kodwa ngendlela ayethuke ngayo, umfana yena akakwazanga ngisho ukukhipha unyembezi. Nempela banqamula imimango bawela imifula nemifudlana nomfokazi lowo, behamba nentombazanyana ezweni elilihlane. Wayengayazi nokuthi ngeyakwabani leyo ntombazane. Kanti futhi akaphindanga wayibona emva kwalokho.

U kukhuIa kuka-okonkwo akufananga nokwabanye abafana. Phela akukho ilia ayelishiyelwe nguyise. Kwakungekho ngisho ingoma kubo. Indaba eyayidumile wukuthi uyise wake wayokhuleka nakusithixo samagquma nemigede, efuna ukuzwa ukuthi kungani engatholi isivuno esijabuIisayo emasimini. 
    Isithixo sasibizwa ngokuthi ngu-Agbala. Abantu babesuka kude naseduze bezokhuleka kuye. Babeza nxa bekhungethwe yisinyama namashwa, noma bexabene nomakhelwane. Abanye babesuke bezohlahla ukuthi ikusasa libaphatheleni nokuzwa ukuthi amathongo akhala ngani. 
    Indlela engena ethempelini lika-Agbala kwakungumgodi owawuseqeleni, othe ukuba mkhudlwana kunomnyango wehhoko lezinkukhu. Abakhonzayo nalabo abasuke bezohlahla babeye bahubazele ngezisu emgedeni baze bayofika endaweni evulekile emnyama bhuqe okuhlezi kuyo u-Agbala. Akukho namunye owayemazi ngeso u-Agbala ngaphandle kwezanusi zakhe. Nokho akukho namunye owayeseke wangena ehuqazela emgedeni owayebuya engathuthumeli ngenxa yamandla ka-Agbala. Isanusi sakhe sa simi ngasemlilweni ongcwele owawubaswe phakathi nendawo emgedeni, okuyiwona owawumemezela intando ka-Agbala. Lo mIilo wawungenalo ilangabi, kwakukhihlike amala.hle nje kuphela. Isingephungephu sezingodo sasikhanyise luvindi lapha kangangoba isanusi sasingabonakali kahle. 
    Khathi simbe indoda yayifika izobhula ukuthi idlozi likayise noma lesihlobo sayo ngabe likhala ngani. Kwakuthiwa lithi lingabizwa idlozi lelo, isithunzi salo sibonakale kalufifi ebumnyameni, kodwa izwi lona lingezwakali. Abanye babeze 




 
basho nokuthi bona bawezwile amathongo endiza futhi eshayisa ngamaphiko ophahleni lomgede. 
    Eminyakeni eyadlulayo, no-Okonkwo esengumfanyana uyise u-Unoka.wake waya ku-Agbala eyobhula. Ngalezo zinsuku isanusi kwabe kuyinkosikazi ebizo layo linguChika. Wayenamakhosi anamandla kakhulu, esabeka. U-Unoka wema ngaphambi kwaso wethula udaba eze ngalo. "Minyaka yonke," esho ngelinosizi, "ngaphambi kokuba ngihlwanyele imbewu yami, ngiye nginikele ngeqhude ku-Ani, ongumnikazi-lizwe. Wumthetho wama-Umuofia lowo. Ngiphinde futhi ngihlabe iqhude, senginikela ku-ifejioku, inkosi yamabhoqongwane. Ngiye ngicabe kahle, ngibabele nxa sekomile. Amabhoqongwane wona ngiwatshala emva kwezimvula zokuqala, futhi kuthi kungaphuma imilibo bese ngiyeseka. Ngiyawahlakula ... " 
    "Khawula:" kusho isanusi ngelihlabayo lenanelwa wubumnyama. "Akukho owone ngakho ku-Agbala nakokhokho bakho. Kunjalo nje uma umuntu engone lutho ezithixweni nakokhokho bakhe isivuno siyoba sihle noma sibe sibi kuye ngomdlandla asebenza ngawo. Wena-ke Unoka waziwa izwe lonke ukuthi wanqamuka izandla; awuvila uyinyoka. Uma omakhelwane bephuma betshethe izimbazo beyocaba emahlathini wena utshala emahlangeni asabangamabhuqu ngoba uvitapha ukucaba. Bawela imifula ngemifula beyolima emasimini anemvundo wena ulibale wukuhlabela amadlozi uthi awabusise izala eselaba yibhuqu. Phindela ekhaya uyosebenza njengendoda." 
    U-Unoka wayelo elandelwe ngamashwa. Kwakubonakala nje ukuthi unedlozi elibi elamdalela umnyama waze waya egodini. Empeleni masithi waze waya ekufeni ngoba phela akazange abe nalo igodi. Wamane wavuvukala umzimba. Lokho-ke kuthathwa njengesinengiso esithixweni somhlaba. Uma umuntu evuvuke esiswini noma ezithweni wayengavunyelwe ukuba ashonele endlini. Wayelahlwa eHlathini Lemimoya Emibi ukuze afele khona. Kuthiwa ikhona-ke indoda yimbe eyayinenkani, okwakuthi lapho 
sebeyilahle ehlathini, itabalazele iphindele ekhaya. Isigcino baze bafike bayibophela emthini khona ehlathini lapho. Lokhu kugula kwakuthathwa njengesiqalekiso. Kanjalo obulewe yikho kwakungamele angcwatshwe emathunjini omhlaba. Wayeyekwa nje abolele ngaphezu komhlabathi. Wayengawutholi umngcwabo wokuqala kanjalo futhi nowesibili. Wayenalelo lishwa-ke naye u-Unoka. Ngesikhathi beyomlahla ehlathini wathabatha umtshingo wakhe kuphela. 
    Enobaba onjalo, u-okonkwo wayengalithathaphi-ke if a ayezosimama ngalo empilweni njengezintanga zakhe? Akukho nqolobane, akukho sicoco ayesishiyelwe nguyise, kwakungekho ngisho nenkosikazi esencane. Phezu kunjalo, wayeseqalile khona esaphila uyise, ukwendlalela ikusasa eliqhakazile. Konke wakuzuza kancane, ngobukhulu ubuhlungu. Kodwa wayezinikele ngempilo yakhe yonke. Phela wayebuswa wuvalo namahloni ngempilo kayise eyabe ihlazisa, kanjalo futhi nokufa kwakhe. 
    Esigodini sakwa-Okonkwo kwabe kunesicebi somnumzane. Wayenezingoma ezintathu, amakhosikazi ayisishiyagololunye kanye nabantwana abangamashumi amathathu. Ibizo lakhe kwakunguNwakibie. Wayesezuze isicoco okungesesibili kweziphakeme kakhulu. Wasebenzela Ie ndoda-ke ukuze athole inhlwayelo yokuqala yamabhoqongwane. 
    Wathatha ukhamba lotshwala kanye neqhude wakusa kuNwakibie. Kwamenywa omakhelwane asebengwevu baba babili kanye namakhulu kaNwakibie omabili bangena kwi-obi yakhe. Wethula isigaxa sekhola nesikapelepele okwajikeleziswa nendlu yonke ukuze kubonwe ngubani nobani. Ekugcineni kwabuyela kuye wayesekudabula maqede wathi: "Unwele olude kithi sonke! Sicela impilo enhle, nabantwana, nesivuno esiyinala, kanye nenjabulo. Yilowo nalowo uyophiwa lokho okumfanele. Unhloyile akayithole indawo azothi coshosho kuyo, kanjalo futhi nokhozi aluthole eyalo. Uma kukhona owenqabela omunye lelo lungelo makanqamuke iphiko."

    Kwathi kungadliwa ikhola leyo u-Okonkwo wayesengenisa utshwala ayekade ebubeke egunjini lendlu. Wathi angabubeka phakathi nendawo wayesekhulekela uNwakibie ethi: "Nna ayi," okungukuthi "Baba wethu".

Nami ngithe angizokhuleka phambi kwakho, ngibuye futhi ngizinxusele. Nokho masiqale ngokwehlisa amathe, ngingakalwethuli udaba lwami."

UNwakibie yena olwakhe walwethula ezintungweni emshayweni. Indodana yakhe encane, okuyiyona eyayincane kunabo bonke endlini yaluthatha ukhamba yaqala ukuthunga utshwala. Inkezo yokuqala yanikwa yena kanye u-Okonkwo ukuze phela asuse ubuthi. Lase liphuza-ke lonke ibandla, kuqalwa ngabadala. Kuthe lapho amadoda esephuze izinkezo noma izimpondo ezimbili noma ezintathu uNwakibie wayesebiza isithembu sakhe. Ngenxa yokuthi abanye babengekho ekhaya, kwangena abane kuphela. "Ngabe akekho yini u-Anasi?" kubuza usokhaya. Aphendula amakhosikazi athi uyeza. Phela u-Anasi lona yinkosikazi yasendlunkulu, ngakho amanye amakhosikazi angephuze kungakaphuzi yena kuqala. ngegama, wayesephindela endlini yakhe. Kanjalo nozakwabo benza njengaye, baphuza bonke ngokulandelana kwabo, base bephindela ezindlini zabo.

    UkwenaneIana ngenhIwayeIo kwakuthatha isikhathi eside ngaphambi kokuba umuntu abe nengobo ethi yena. KwakungehIukene Iokho nokutheIa izinhIamvu zamabeIe esakeni eIivuzayo. Unina nodadewabo ababili basebenza kanzima nabo beIekeIeIa kepha-ke bona babetshaIa izilimo zabesimame, njengezindumba, ukhokho, kanye nomdumbuIa. Amabhoqongwane okuyiwona nkosi yezidIo, ayelinywa ngamadoda. 
    KuIowo nyaka u-Okonkwo athatha ngawo amakhuIu ayisishiyagaIombili amabhoqongwane kuNwakibie, Kwakungunyaka omubi ngendIeIa engazange ibonwe ezweni. Akukho nje okwakwenzeka ngesikhathi sakho. Izinto zazishesha okanye zephuze kakhuIu. Kwakungathi izwe Iikhungethwe ngumsangano. Imvula yokwenduIeIisa yephuza ukuna, kanti kwathi noma seIe~wasa, yana isikhashana nje. Ilanga eliyisigayegaye Iangqongqisa konke okuIuhIaza. UmhIaba wawusushisa sengathi k~basiwe. Okwamamabhoqongwane okwase kumilile kwaba" sengathi kade kosiwa. U-Okonkwo wayetshaIe ngazo kanye Iezo mvuIa zokwenduIeIisa. WayesatshaIe amakhuIu amane embewu ngenkathi Iinqamuka ukuna, kungena isomiso. Emini Ialize Iishone ebuka phezuIu esibhakabhakeni ngethemba Iokuthi angahle abone amafu emvuIa. Ngisho ebusuku wayevuka 




 
aqwashe, ethatha ebeka. Ngakusasa uma ephindela emasimini wayefike abingelelwe yimilibo ebunileyo. Kwakwehlula noma esemboza izithombo zakhe ngamahlamvu otsiligwane. Lalithi lishona amahlahla abe esome abayizinkohlo. Wayesemi ngokuwashintsha nsuku zonke, elokhu ethandaze lokho, enxusa imvula. Kodwa labalela kwaphela amasonto ayisishiyagalombili, emasimini kwasha khothe. 
    Abanye abalimi babengakahlwayeli. Kwakungovilavoco labo ababephike ngokulayezela ukuthi basazoyocaba kuqala. Ngalo nyaka babonakala beyizihlakaniphi. Babezwelana nomakhelwane baze banikine amakhanda, kanti ngengaphakathi bayasho bathi nakho phela ukuba ngamaqhalaqhala, sebenza sengathi bona basheshe basibona isimo kanti babephethwe ubuvila. 
    Kwathi ekubuyeni kwezimvula, u-Okonkwo watshala leyo mbewu eyayisasele. Waziduduza ngento eyodwa yo: 
Imbewu ayeyitshala lingakomisi izulu kwabe kungeyakhe eyivune ngonyaka odlule. Amakhulu ayesishiyagalombiJi ayewenane kuNwakibie namakhulu amane ayewenanelwe ngumngani kayise ayengakathintwa. Wazimisela-ke ukuba aphinde erne ngazo zombili futhi. 
Kodwa isimo sasibheda. Izulu lavele lathela uzamcolo. 
Layidliva imini nobusuku nsuku zonke, lemukisa wena bhoqongwane, wenani. Iziqu zemithi zazisimbuka zibheke phezulu. Izwe lonke laphenduka izindonga. Kwaya ngokuya yancipha futhi imvula, kodwa alizange lise. Yakhula yabhangazela imilibo, kodwa wonke umuntu wayazi ukuthi uma lingazange lihlabe ilanga leyo milibo ngeke ibekele. Nembala isivuno sangalowo nyaka sasidabukisa kuhle komngcwabo. Abanye abalimi babekhala ezimathonsi bebona amabhoqongwana esebolile. Indoda yimbe yamane yazibophela egatsheni lomuthi ngehiya layo yazilengisa yafa. 
    Njalo nxa ekhumbula lowo nyaka u-Okonkwo wayemane avevezele wonke umzimba. Wayemangala nje ukuthi yena wasizwa yini ukuba angasale esethela. Wayazi ukuthi uyisilwi esesabekayo kodwa isimo sezinto ngalowo nyaka 
sasingayephula ngisho inhliziyo yebhubesi. "Ngoba ngasinda ngalowo nyaka," wayeye ezwakale esesho omdala, "sengiyosinda ngisho ngihlaselwe ubunzima obungakanani." Lokho kwaba yinto embusa ezinzulwini zezibilini zakhe. 
    UYise u-Unoka, owayesexhwalile ngaleso sikhathi, wathi kuye ngesikhathi sekuvunwa: "Ungalahli ithemba. Ngiyazi ngeke ulilahle ithemba. Wen a ungusibindi-gidi! Akukho okunganqoba labo abathi: yize uvalo, inqobo yisibindi. Okunzima kakhulu wukuba indoda ishikashikeke yehluleke iyodwana." Wayenjalo u-Unoka ezinsukwini zakhe zokugcina. Ukugula nokuguga kwakusengathi kumenza ukuba akhulumele futhi. Wayecasuka kuthi akazibulale u-Okonkwo.

Kwase kusondela Umkhosi Wokunyathela Uswela e-Umuofia, bonke abantu sebewubheke ngabomvu. Kwakuyisikhathi leso sokubonga ku-Ani, isithixo somhlabathi kanye nenala. U-Ani wayaziswa emphakathini ukwedlula ngisho nOlna yisiphi esinye isithixo. Kwakunguyena mahluleli omkhulu mayelana nokuziphatha okuyikhonakhona kobuntu. Kanti futhi wayesondelene kakhulu nalabo asebedlulile emhlabeni, amathongo amakhulu esizwe. 
    UMkhosi Woselwa wawenziwa minyaka yonke ngaphambi kokuba kuvunwe, kubongwa ngawo isithixo somhlabathi nenala kanye namathongo esizwe. Wawungeke ulokothe udle aInabhoqongwane amasha kungakagujwa 10 mkhosi, kunikelwe ngamabhoqongwane emadIozini kuqala. Wonke uwonke,abesilisa nabesifazane, abadala nabancane, babewubheka ngabomvu 10 mkhosi ngoba yiwona phela onquma ukuqala konyaka omusha. Ngobusuku bokugcina ngaphambi komkhosi kwakulahlwa onke amabhoqongwane amadala yilabo abasenawo. Phela unyaka omusha kumele uqale ngokweshwama okusha, okumnandi, hhayi okudala kwanyakomunye. Zonke izimbiza zokupheka, nezigubhu zose1wa kanye nemicakulo nezingqoko kwakuhIanzwa kahle, ikakhulukazi izigqulo zokugqula amabhoqongwane. Pmhluzi wamabhoqongwane nemifino kwakuwukudla okuphambili okudliwa ngomkhosi. Kwakuphekwa kubengangamanzi okuphala izikhumba, kwehlule abomndeni kuze kwehlule ngisho izihambeli imbala. Kwakunendaba ababevame ukuyixoxa yendoda ethile eyayinothile, eyethula phambi kwezihambeli zayo inqwaba yamabhoqongwane 




 
eyayingangentaba. Ohlezi ngapha kwayo wayengaboni ukuthi kukhonani ngale. Kwaze kwabantambama impela lapho othile abona khana abasemzini abafike kudliwa, bafika nabo basina bazibethela. Kwaba yikhona exhawulana nabasemzini, kubingelelwana. Ngaleso sikhathi kwase kukuncane ukudla okwakusasele. UMkhasi Wakunyathela Uselwa kwakuwumkhosi wokuzithakozisa kulo lonke elase-Umuofia. Yileya ndoda enesandla esiqinile, ngokusho kwama-Ibo, yayilindeleke ukuba imeme izindimbane zezivakashi ezisuka kude naseduze. U-Okonkwo yena wayemema zonke izihlabo zasemakhweni akhe. Njengoba wayesenamakhwe amathathu njena, kusobala ukuthi kwakuye kufike izivakashi eziningi kakhulu. 
    Yize kunjalo, u-Okonkwo wayengakwesaseli njengabanye ukugubhana nemikhosi. Wayedla yena,kanti futhi nakokuphuzwaya wayefika impela ngoba isigubhu esikhulu sotshwala wayesishayela ekhanda eyedwa. Into nje kwakumcasula ukuhlala izinsuku ngezinsuku kununyuzwa. Wayecabanga ukuthi ngabe kungcono kabi ukuba usemasimini akhe, uyasebenza. 
Kwase kusele'izinsuku ezintathu kube ngumkhosi. 
Amakhosikazi ka-Okonkwo ayeselungise kahle ekhaya, esinda ngensoyi, izindlu sekuyizibuka. 
    Zazihlotshiswe kahle ngemidwebo ephuzi nemhlaphe kanye neluhlaza ngokujiyile. Emva kwalokho azihlobisa wona ngemidwebo yokhuni kanye nezithambe ezimnyama lapha eziswini nasemhlane. Abantwana nabo babehlotshiswe kahle ikakhulukazi izinwele ezazigundwe amaphethini amahle. Omathathu amakhosikazi ayengawuhlanganisi umlomo ngezihlobo ezazimenyiwe, nezingane zazisizakele zizototaswa ngoninalume nezinye izihlabo zasemakhayakonina. U-Ikemefuna naye wayejabule edelile. Wabana ukuthi kuleli uMkhosi Woselwa uyindabamlonyeni ukwedlula kwelakubo. Kanti vele kuncane kakhulu ayesakukhumbula ngelakubo. 
    Kusenjalo, lase lidumile izulu kusokhaya. U-Okonkwo awayelokhu ehla enyuka enxulumeni lakhe, waze wakuthola 
azobhodlela kukho njengoba ayethukuthele eqhuma nje: 
"Ubani obulele isibhanana sami?" wabuza esebhavumulisa akwebhubesi. Kwathula ovunguzayo ekhaya. "Ngithi ngubani obulele 10 muthi? Niyizithulu okanye niyizimungulu?" Empeleni umuthi lowo wawuziphilela saka. Umfazi ka-Okonkwo wesibili wayemane nje wakha amacembe ambalwa efuna ukugoqa ngawo ukudla. Nempela achaze kanjalo. Kanti useyinyathele emsileni ku-Okonkwo. Wayemdinda ngenduku njalo! Wamshiya lapho ekhala ezimathonsi kanye nendodakazi yakhe eyodwa. Amakhosikazi akhe ehluleka nokumlamula. Ayegcina ngakho ukumkhalela ethi: "Sekwenele phela, baba!" nakho lokho ekusho emele ekudeni. 
Wathi angabhodla ufeleba, wayesehamba eyozingela. 
Wayenesibhamu esidala ayesenzelwe ngumkhandi ohlakaniphile, okwasekuyiminyaka afika ezokwakha lapha e-Umuofia. Nanxa u-Okonkwa ayeyingwazi ehlonishwayo, kepha wabe engel ana iphisi. Empeleni wayengakaze abulale ngisho igundane ngalesi sibhamu sakhe. Ngakho kwathi lapho ethi u-Ikemefuna akalethe isibhamu sakhe, 10 nkosikazi awayekade eshaywa wangunangunaza amazwana ayiziswana, ngezibhamu ezingadubuli nyamazane. Kanti ungunangunaza nje, uyezwa u-Okonkwo. Wanikela egunjini ngasa leso sikhathi, wadumela isibhamu esabe sihlohliwe, wuphuma naso wasiqondisa ngqo kumkakhe owayesatatabuka eyokweqa udonga Iwenqolobane. Wasidonsa isicupho, sadubula isibhamu, kwavimbanisa umsindo wokuduma kwaso kanye nokukhala kwesimame nezingane. Wasilahla phansi isibhamu wagxumela enqolobaneni, wamthola umkakhe engumfunzana laphaya phansi, ethuke eqhaqhazela, kodwa ngenhlahla, wabe engalimele. Umnumzane waphefumula ngokukhulu ukukhululeka wabe esethatha isibhamu sakhe ehamba. 
    Ngaphandle kwalesi sigameko, usuku 10Mkhosi Iwagujwa ngenkulu intokozo emndenini ka-Okonkwo. Ekuseni ngenkathi enza umnikelo kwabaphansi ngamabhoqongwane amasha namafutha, wabanxusa ukuba bamlondaloze kahle

kwenkundla, ngemvana nje kwezibukeli. Kwakuhlala kuhlale bese kusuka ezimbili ziphethe amahlamvu esundu zigijime zijikeleze inkundla ziqhelisa izihlwele ngokubhula phansi ngaphambi kwazo ngamahlahla lawo, kuthi abanenkani babhulwe imilenze kanye nezinyawo ukuze bahlehlele emuva.

Abanye-ke babemi ngezinyawo ngaphandle kwalelo dlanzana elabe lisheshe lafika lathola izindawo zokuhlala ezabe zakhiwe ngezingodo ezazigaxwe ezigxotsheni eziyizimbaxa.

Ezinsukwini ezejwayelekile amakhosikazi asemasha afuna abantwana ayeza afike ahlale emthunzini wawo.

Kwaba sengathi kade uthululelwe esikhurnbeni sesigubhu esidonswe saqina ngqi. Kwaqala ngqa ukuba abantu bathole nethuba lokujeqeza eceleni babone ukuthi bahiezi nobani.

    "Yiqiniso elimsulwa lelo, mngani wami. Namanje anginarnlomo, angazi nokuthi yinto engingayixoxa ngithini lena." 
    "Cha, unedlozi eIikhulu, mhIobo wami. Injani kodwa indodakazi yami, u-Ezinma?" 
    "Ukhombise obukhuIu ubungcono muva nje, MhIawumbe useyophila." 
    "Nami ngicabanga kanjalo. Konje useneminyaka emingaki manje?"

    "Umthandazo wami omkhulu wukuthi aphile," kwasho u-Ekwefi edonsa umoya.

Umhlaba wawunqume ukuthi bayisinengiso ezweni ngakho kumele babhujiswe noma baginyiswe igabade. Uma isizwe singayithobeli intando yesithixo somhlabathi ngokubajezisa, lokho kwakuyodala imikhokha emibi ezweni lonke, hhayi kuphela kulabo abonile. Kakade izwi labadala lithi nxa umunwe ugcobhoze emafutheni, wona iminwe yonke esandleni. Lokho kusafana nje nokuthi zifa ngamvunye.

Waqala-ke umshikashika wokulungiselela ukubuyela komndeni ka-Okonkwo emuva. Lokho kwakuzokwenzeka emva kwezimvula zehlobo. Wayengafisa u-Okonkwo ukuba asheshe kunalokho ukuphindela emuva khona ayezofike akhe umuzi wakhe zingakanqamuki izimvula kodwa lokho kwakuzosho ukuthi usifingqile isigwebo sakhe seminyaka eyisikhombisa. Wayengazimisele ukwenzenialo. Walinda ngesineke-ke kwaze kwanqamuka izimvula. 
    Imvula yayina kancane nie. Yaqala iyimikhizo enganakekile kodwa yaya ngokuqina kwaze kwaba yishihlambi esibonakalayo impela. Kwesinye isikhathi ilanga lalithi ukuvela likhanye kuyo imiklezo yemvula bese kuphephetha umoya opholile. Kwakuyimvula enhle elula, eyimiklezo. Kwaqala manje kwavela uthingo Iwenkosazana. Kokunye zazivela zibe mbiIi, kube sengathi unina nendodakazi yakhe. Olunye Iwalugqama kahle santombazana encane enhle, olunye lube luvindi sengathi yinkosikazi endala. Uthingo lwenkosazana lwalubizwa ngokuthi yinhIwathi yasemkhathini. 
    U-Okonkwo wabiza isithembu sakhe ezositshela ukuthi asil ungiselele umgidi. "Kumele ngibabonge abantu basekhayakomame ngaphambi kokuba ngihambe," sekusho yena. 
    U-Ekwefi wayesenayo ikhasava eyayisale nyakenye ensimini yakhe. Lana amanye amakhosikazi amabili wona ayengasenayo. Lokho akusho ukuthi ayevilapha, wukuthi nie babenemindeni emikhulu ngakho iminingi imilomo okumele bayondle. Kwakulindelekile-ke ukuba kube ngu-Ekwefi oletha ikhasava yomcimbi. Unina kaNwoye kanye no-Ojiugu bona

babezolungisa okunye njengenhlanzi efusiwe, amafutha esundu, kanye nopelepele wesobho. U-Okonkwo yena wayezobhekana nenyama namabhoqongwane.

wakwenza sekwedlule izinsuku eziyisiphohlongo balwa. Phela lokho kwabangwa wukuthi akasheshanga ukufa u-Oduche. Kwaze kwaba wusuku lwesikhombisa ngenkathi ukufa kumenela. Nokho amaKhrestu amotha kubelungu ngale ngozi bona base bethuma oKotma babo ukuyombamba. Wafakwa ejele kanye nabo bonke abaholi bomndeni wakhe. Nangempela wathi angafa u-oduche, u-Aneto wedluliselwa e-Umuru wayolengiswa khona. Abanye bona badedelwa kodwa kuze kube namuhla lokhu basakhungathekile, abanamlomo abangasichazela ngawo ngokuhlupheka abahlushwa ngakho. 
    Kwaphela isikhathi eside emva kwale ngxoxo, la madoda ewuhlabe inhlali omabili, edla amathambo ekhanda. 

ISAHLUKO 21 

Baningi abesilisa nabesifazane lapha e-Umuofia ababengalubuki ngaso linye no-Okonkwo lolu hlelo olusha ezweni. Khona kungephikiswe ukuthi inkolo yomlungu yayingehlukene neyezinhlanya, kodwa-ke wayesebuye wakha nesitolo umntanomlungu lona. Kwaqala-ke ukuba izinto ebezinganakiwe njengamafutha esundu kanye nekheneli kube yizinto zenani elikhulu, yaqala-ke nemali ukungena igelezisa okwamanzi lapha e-Umuofia. Kanti nakuyo nje inkolo, babeya ngokwanda abathi qhabo-bo, likhona iqiniso elingephikiswe kule nkolo. Iqiniso likhona nanxa okuningi kuwubuhlanya nje. 
Ukubuka izinto ngalolu hlobo kwabhebhezelwa nguMnu. 
Brown, umfundisi omhlophe, owayengafuni nokuzwa ukuba amakholwa achukuluze isizwe. Linye ilunga elabe lingakhuzeki. Lowo kwakungu-Enoch, owayezalwa yindoda eyayikholelwa ekukhonzeni izinyoka. Kwezwakala ngabasiki bebunda ukuthi u-Enoch ndini wayebulale inhlwathi yabaphansi wayidla, okwabangela ukuba uyise amqalekise. 
    UMnu. Brown washumayela ngokuba abantu bangavumeli izinhliziyo ngale ndlela. Yonke into ingenzeka, esho kubalandeli bakhe ababekhombisa umdlandla omkhulu. Wagcizelela nokho ukuthi akuzona zonke izinto ezifanele ukwenziwa. Kanjalo baqala ukumhlonipha uMnu .. Brown phakathi kwesizwe ngoba wayengathathi ngamawala okholweni lwakhe. Waba ngumngani wezikhulu phakathi kwesizwe. Kwathi lusuku lumbe evakashele esigodini esingumakhelwane waphiwa izinyo lendlovu elabe libazwe kahle, okwaba wuphawu lwesithunzi kanye nesikhundla esiphakeme ayecatshangelwa kuso. Akuzanga nje kuphela abasha ukuzofunda, abanye basebeqinile impela sebeneminyaka engamashumi amathuthu noma ngaphezulu. Babevukela emasimini ekuseni, baze baye esikoleni ntambama. Dukuduku wezwa abantu sebenanela ukuthi umuthi womlungu uyashesha ukusebenza. Isikole sikaMnu. Brown sasheshe sathela izithelo Emveni koku£Unda izinyangana ezimbalwa, wawuzwa sekuthiwa umuntu useyisithunywa senkantolo, noma usengumabhalane khona enkantolo. Labo abafunda isikhashana esithe thuthu bagcina sebengothisha. Kanjalo ezweni lase-Umuofia zathi chithi saka izisebenzi ezazisebenza esivinini seNkosi. Kwaqhibuka amasonto ngisho ezigodini ezingomakhelwane. Nakhona £Uthi ukwakhiwa kwamasonto kwalandelwa wukwakhiwa kwezikole. Eyabayinhle kunazo zonke, ngokueabanga kwakhe, yileyo abayilwa nesizwe sama-Isike. Kulezo zinsuku u-Okudo wayesadla amabele. U-Okudo wayephuma phambili kulabo abakwazi ukuhuba amahubo empi. Yena wayengesona isilwi kodwa ngezwi lakhe nje qha, wayekwazi ukufaka umoya emabuthweni azizwe esengamabhubesi. 
    "Sazalwa nabanye, namhIa sesiguga nabanye," kueabanga u-Okonkwo ekhumbula lezomini. "Ama-Isike ayofa engazange ayikhohlwe indlela esawagwazisa okwebheee ngayo kuleyo mpi. Sabulala abayishumi nambili ngakubo kanti ngakithi 
kwafa ababili kuphela. Kwathi lingakapheli iviki lesine base beeeia uxolo. Lezo kwakuyizinsuku lapho amadoda kwakusengamadoda, hhayi indaba yokudlala:' 
    Esaeabanga ngalezi zinto wayizwa inhlabamkhosi ishaya igekle ngaphandle, kude Ie. Walalelisisa, nebala walizwa kaneane izwi lenhlabamkhosi. Kodwa lalizwakalela ekudeni. Waphenduka embhedeni, wezwa ukuthi umhlane wakhe ubuhlungu. Wagedla amazinyo. Inhlabamkhosi yayisisondela kaneane, kaneane manje. nembala yaze yedlula ngasemzini wakhe .. 
    "Incinga enkulu kuleli lase-Umuofia, yileli gwala elingu-Egonwanne. Ngalobu bugagu bakhe uyakwazi ukuphendula umlilo ube umlotha obandayo. Uma sekukhuluma yena, amadoda kuba sengathi atheniwe. Ukuba abazange babunake lobu buhlakani bakhe obufuze obamanina eminyakeni emihlanu eyedule, ngabe izinto azizange zihambe ngale ndlela." Waphinda futhi wadla imihlathi. "Kusasa uzobe esebatshela ukuthi obaba abakaze bayilwe 'impi yokusolwa. 'Uma beke Bamlalela ngiyobashiya benjalo, ngihambe ngedwa ngiyoziphindiselela. " 
    Laphinda futhi izwi lenhlabamkhosi lasholo ph ansi ngenxa yokuthi yayisikude kanjalo futhi ibanga laselenza ingekle nalo lizwakale kaneane, lalingasahlabi. Waphinda futhi u-Okonkwo waphenduka kulolu hlangothi walala ngaloluya. Ubuhlungu ayebuzwa kwabasengathi buyamkitaza. "Ake alinge nje u-Egonwanne akhulume' ngempi yokusolwa' kusasa ngiyovele ngimkhombise umhIane wami 10 kanye nekhanda:' Waphinde wadla imihlathi. 
    Lathi liqeda ukuthi phasha ilanga, kwabe sekugcwele enkundleni yasendalini. U-Obierika wayesalinde elawini lakhe ngenkathi kufika u-Okonkwo ezombiza. Wagaxa isikhwama sakhe kanye nengxiwa kaeelemba ehlombe waphuma wazohambisana no-Okonkwo. Indlu ka-Obierika yayiseduze nendlela ngakho wayebabona bonke abedlulayo beya enkundleni yasendalini. Nangalokhu kusa, baningi abedlulayo ayesebingelelene nabo.

    U-Obierika no-Gkonkwo bafika enkundlemi yasendalini abantu bengasebaningi, sebengangoboya bendlovu. Kodwa futhi izindimbane zazisalokhu zithelekile zivela kuzo zonke izigodi zase-Umuofia eziyisishiyagalolunye. Wezwa efudumala u-Gkonkwo lapho ebona izinkumbi ngezinkumbi zabantu. Kodwa munye umuntu ayefuna ukumbona; leyo ndoda enlimi olumnadi ayelwesaba futhi elwenyanya. 
"Uyambona?" ebuza ku-Obierika. "Ubani?" 
    "U-Egonwanne," kusho u-Okonkwo amehlo eth,.ungatha yonke indawo, eya Ie nale endalini. Iningi lamadoda lalihlezi ezikhumbeni zezimbuzi. Abambalwa babehlezi ezigqikini ababefike nazo. 
    "Qha," kuphendula u-Obierika, naye ephosa amehlo ezixukwini. "Yebo! Nanguya. Uhlezi ngaphansi kwesihlahla sokolweni. Wenqene ukuthi angahle aphumelele ukusinganda ukuba singayiphaki impi?" 
    "Ngimenqenile? Anginamsebenzi nokuthi uzokwenzani ngani. Mina nje ngiyamenyanya, kanjalo futhi nalabo abamlalelayo. Uma kunjani nga ngingamane ngiyilwe ngingedwa." 
    Babekhulumela phezulu ngoba kwakuhhomuzela wonke umuntu wawungathi yisidleke sezinyosi. 
    "Ngizolinda aze akhulume," kucabanga u-Okonkwo, "bese kubayikhona ngikhulumayo." 
    Kodwa wazi ngani ukuthi inkulumo yakhe izobe iphikisana nempi?" kubuza u-Obierika emva kwesikhashana. 
    "Ngoba ngiyamazi ukuthi uyigwala," kuchaza u-Okonkwo. U-Obierika akabange esakuzwa konke okwakushiwo ngu-Okonkwo ngoba kukhona owamqhweba ehlombe engemuva, wayesephenduka ukuze akwazi ukuxhawula nokubuza impilo kubangani bakhe abahlanu noma abayisithupha. U-Okonkwo yena akazange abheke emuva yize ayewazi amazwi ukuthi awobani. Wayengenaso yena isikhathi sokubingelelana nabantu. Yize kunjalo enye kula madoda yamthinta, ibuza ngempilo yabomndeni wakhe. 
"Bebesatotoba," ephendula nje ngokunganaki. 
    Indoda yokuqala eyabeka izwi kuma-Umuofia kwaba ngu-Okika, ongomunye walabo ababekade beboshiwe. U-Okika wabe eyindoda emadodeni, futhi eyimbongi, Nokho wayengenayo imbodlongo yezwi okufanele lisetshenziswe yisikhulumi sokuqala, elizokwazi ukuthulisa izihlwele. Ngu-Onyeka owayenezwi elinjalo. Nebala kwacelwa yena ukuba abingelele amabandla ngaphambi kokuba u-Okika akhulume. 
    "Umuofia kwenu!" (okungukuthi siyanibingelela mabandla ase-Umuofia), esho ephakamisa isandla sokunxele enza sengathi ududula umoya ngezandla. "Yea!" kuduma inkundla, amabandla ephendula, evuma. 
    "Umuofia kwenu," ephinda futhi ebhodla kakhulu ebheka ngapha nangapha. Zaphinda futhi izihlwele zaphendula ngokuthi, "Yaa!" 
    Kwathi nya kwasengathi kukhona othele amanzi aqandayo emlilweni obuvutha amalangabi. Wasukuma-ke u-Okika wabingelela ibandla kane wayeseqala ukukhuluma, "Nonke niyazi ukuthi kungani silapha, esikhundleni sokuba ngabe sakha izinqolobane zethu noma siduza izindlu silungise imizi yethu. Ubaba wayejwayele ukuthi 'nxa ubona idwi ligxumagxuma emini kabha, ubokwazi ukuthi kukhona okuzingela impilo yalo'. Kanjalo kuthe lapho nginibona niqhamuka emagumbini omane nizothutheleka kule ndawo ekuseni kusa, kungikhanyele ukuthi kukhona okuzingela impilo yenu." Wathi ukuhlaba ikhefu, esagwinya amathe, wayesebuye eqhubeka. 
    "Zonke izithixo zethu ziyakhala. Ngisho u-Idernili ukhihla isililo. Ngisho u-Ogwugwu uyakhala. Kanjalo no-Agbala ukhihla isililo kanye nezinye izithixo.     "Yimbizo enkulu lena. Asikho esinye isizwe esingazishaya isifuba sithi sinezihlwele kanye namaqhawe angaphezu kwalana. Kodwa siphelele sonke na? Ngiyabuza. Ngabe onke amadodana ethu ahlanganyele kunye nathi njengoba silapha?" Kwezwakala ukuvungama okwakusholo phansi esixukwini.

Abazange bakhiphe imiphefumulo yabafowabo. Kodwa phela babengekho abelungu phakathi kwabo. Ngakho namhlanje kumele senze lokho obaba ababengekulokothe. Ububi kumele sibusiphule nezimpande zabo, sibulahlele ngaphandle. Uma abafowethu beehema nesitha nabo kumele sibashaye sibabhuqe. Lokho kumele sikwenze njengamanje.     Laba ababelindile kungathi yizikhomololo, bagxuma basakazeka nenkundla, kwaba wukuehitheka komhIangano. Wema u-Okonkwo ebheke indoda ayeseyieoboshisile.     Kwathi lapho befika emthini okwakulenga kuwo isidumbu sika-Okonkwo, bema sengathi bashaywe umbani wezulu. 
    "Mhlawurnbe la madoda ohamba nawo angasisiza ukuba simethule siyornngcwaba." kusho u-Obierika. "Sithumele abantu bezizwe abakhele esinye isigodi ukuba bazosisiza, kodwa bangahle bephuze kakhulu." 
UNdabazabantu washintsha ngaso leso sikhathi.

Yilokho-ke sinxusa abantu bakho ukuba basehlisele yena, ngoba bona bangabantu bezizwe." 
    "Nizornngcwaba njenganoma yimuphi omunye umuntu?" kuphenya yena futhi uNdabazabantu. 
    "Phinde! Asisakwazi ukurnngcwaba. Angangcwatshwa ngabezizwe kuphela. Sizobakhokhela aban.tu bakho ngokusingcwabela yena. Uma esengcwatshiwe siyokwazi ukuphetha amasiko akithi maqondana naye. Siyokwenza nornhlatshelo wokuhlarnbulula urnhlabathi osungcofekile." 
    U-Obierika oweyakade elokhu egqolozele isidumbu somngani wakhe esasilenga, wajikela kuNdabazabantu wesifunda, wakhuluma naye ngokukhulu ukufutheka wathi,

    UNdabazabantu wathukuthela waklwela ebusweni wabomvu tebhu. Wawadonsa ngendlebe amadoda ethi urna engarnkhiphi u-Okonkwo uzowavalela esikidi ngothi lwawo. Aqala ukuvungazela amadoda kwathi ekugcineni waphinda futhi u-Obierika wakhulurna.

"Le ndoda kwakuyiqhawe lamaqhawe lapha e-Umuofia. Wena umphoqelele ekubeni agcine esezibulele. Ngikhuluma ,nje usezongewatshiswa okwenja ... " Akazange esakwazi ukuqhubeka. Izwi lakhe laqala ukugedezela, wagcwalelana kangangoba amazwi awabange esakwazi ukuphuma emlonyeni wakhe.

    Wasuka lapho uNdabazabantu zaya, ehamba namasotsha amathathu noma amane. Eminyakeni eminingi esebenza nzima ezama ukufaka impueuko ezingxenyeni ezahlukene e-Afrika, wayesefunde lukhulu. Okunye kwalokho wukuthi uNdabazabantu wesifunda akumele azigaxe ezintweni ezingasho lutho nezizomkhipha isithunzi njengokwethula isidumbu somuntu ozibulele emthini. Phela kuningi okunye okumele kufakwe kuleli bhuku, ngakho kusemqoka ukuba kungalitshalwa yimininingwane ewundendende. Ngisho isihloko sebhuku wayesesikhethile.
